Mr Samir Modi, Founder and Managing Director of Modicare Limited is an intuitive entrepreneur, constantly striving to bring new and radical ideas to life. He is also the Managing Director of Modi Enterprises founded by his grandfather, Rai Bahadur Gujarmal Modi in 1933.
Under the leadership of his father Late Mr KK Modi, Modi Enterprises, a Rs 10,000 crore conglomerate became one of biggest Indian businesses.
Mr Samir Modi serves on the board of various organisations in several capacities, which include - Executive Director, Godfrey Phillips India Ltd; Director, Indofil Industries Ltd; Founder & President, 24Seven Convenience Stores and Founder & Managing Director, Colorbar Cosmetics, Founder & Vice- Chairman, Modicare Foundation
Mr Modi is the President of the Confederation of Asia Pacific Chambers of Commerce and Industry (CACCI). He also a member of the FICCI National Executive Committee, FICCI Steering Committee and NACS Asia Pacific Committee (National Association of Convenience Stores).
An alumnus of the famed Harvard Business School, Mr ModiтАЩs stint in the US has imbued him with a global perspective and a multicultural approach to work. During his overseas stay, the success of Indians worldwide amazed him. while he witnessed Indians struggling in their own country. This led him to believe that the major barrier was capital investment and the only way to replicate the success in India was via financial independence. Recognising the immense potential of Direct Selling, he decided to launch his own Direct Selling Company in India
Continuing his family tradition of nation-building at the youthful age of 25, in March 1996 Mr Samir Modi launched IndiaтАЩs first Direct Selling Company, Modicare, with the vision of Giving тАШAzadiтАЩ to every Indian. Today Modicare is one of IndiaтАЩs leading direct selling company and is giving Azadi to millions of people.
He also shouldered the responsibility of continuing his familyтАЩs philanthropic tradition by setting up the Modicare Foundation in 1996. The Foundation undertakes extensive work in HIV/AIDS Awareness and gender-related issues while working proactively for childrenтАЩs education.
Understanding contemporary consumer behaviour and trends in the Indian cosmetic industry, he established Colorbar Cosmetics in 2004 to rival international brands. Today, it is the third-largest cosmetics brand in an industry dominated by international giants.
Another brainchild of Mr Samir Modi is the 24Seven Convenience Stores тАУ IndiaтАЩs first-of-its-kind, round-the-clock convenience retail chain, launched in 2005. Currently, it has more than 100 stores in Delhi-NCR, Chandigarh, Mohali and Panchkula.
